TRUE

[@穿戴时装]
#IFONE
EQUAL $SCRIPTPARAM(1) 
EQUAL $SCRIPTPARAM(2) 
#ACT
BREAK

#IF
!LARGE <$TABLE(SZ_<$SCRIPTPARAM(1)>).<$SCRIPTPARAM(2)>> 0
#ACT
SENDMSG 19 尚未激活该时装
BREAK

#IF
EQUAL $SCRIPTPARAM(1) WQ
EQUAL $JOB 战士
#ACT
SETSECRETINFO $USERNAME $CustomValue(54) $SCRIPTPARAM(3)
ChangeCustomValue 53 = $SCRIPTPARAM(3)
CLEARVAR S$武器穿戴 8
SENDMSG 19 穿戴成功
GOTO @<$SCRIPTPARAM(6)>
GOTO @临时属性
BREAK

#IF
EQUAL $SCRIPTPARAM(1) WQ
EQUAL $JOB 法师
#ACT
SETSECRETINFO $USERNAME $CustomValue(54) $SCRIPTPARAM(4)
ChangeCustomValue 53 = $SCRIPTPARAM(4)
CLEARVAR S$武器穿戴 8
SENDMSG 19 穿戴成功
GOTO @<$SCRIPTPARAM(6)>
GOTO @临时属性
BREAK

#IF
EQUAL $SCRIPTPARAM(1) WQ
EQUAL $JOB 道士
#ACT
SETSECRETINFO $USERNAME $CustomValue(54) $SCRIPTPARAM(5)
ChangeCustomValue 53 = $SCRIPTPARAM(5)
CLEARVAR S$武器穿戴 8
SENDMSG 19 穿戴成功
GOTO @<$SCRIPTPARAM(6)>
GOTO @临时属性
BREAK

#IF
EQUAL $SCRIPTPARAM(1) YF
#ACT
SETSECRETINFO $USERNAME $SCRIPTPARAM(3) $CustomValue(53)
ChangeCustomValue 54 = $SCRIPTPARAM(3)
CLEARVAR S$衣服穿戴 8
SENDMSG 19 穿戴成功
GOTO @<$SCRIPTPARAM(6)>
GOTO @临时属性
BREAK

#IFONE
EQUAL $SCRIPTPARAM(1) CGDD
EQUAL $SCRIPTPARAM(1) HDDD
#ACT
ADDFH 0 3 $SCRIPTPARAM(3) -67 -45 
ChangeCustomValue 52 = $SCRIPTPARAM(3)
CLEARVAR S$顶戴穿戴 29
SENDMSG 19 穿戴成功
GOTO @<$SCRIPTPARAM(4)>
GOTO @临时属性
BREAK

#IF
EQUAL $SCRIPTPARAM(1) ZJ
#ACT
CHANGEMODE 45 $SCRIPTPARAM(3)
ChangeCustomValue 55 = $SCRIPTPARAM(3)
CLEARVAR S$足迹穿戴 8
SENDMSG 19 穿戴成功
GOTO @<$SCRIPTPARAM(6)>
GOTO @临时属性
BREAK

[@卸下时装]
#IF
EQUAL $SCRIPTPARAM(1) WQ
#ACT

MOV N$由卸下来 1
CLEARVAR S$武器穿戴 8
SENDMSG 19 卸下成功
GOTO @<$SCRIPTPARAM(6)>
GOTO @临时属性
BREAK

#ACT

MOV N$由卸下来 1
CLEARVAR S$衣服穿戴 8
SENDMSG 19 卸下成功
GOTO @<$SCRIPTPARAM(6)>
GOTO @临时属性
BREAK

EQUAL $SCRIPTPARAM(1) HDDD
#ACT

ChangeCustomValue 52 = 0
MOV N$由卸下来 1

SENDMSG 19 卸下成功

GOTO @临时属性
BREAK

#ACT

GOTO @<$SCRIPTPARAM(6)>

[@给时装升星]
#IF
SMALL <$TABLE(SZ_<$SCRIPTPARAM(1)>).<$SCRIPTPARAM(2)>> 1
#ACT
SENDMSG 19 您尚未获得<$STR(S$时装名)>
BREAK

#IF
!SMALL <$TABLE(SZ_<$SCRIPTPARAM(1)>).<$SCRIPTPARAM(2)>> 7
#ACT
SENDMSG 19 <$STR(S$时装名)>已升至满星
BREAK

#IF
!SMALL <$ITEMVALSUM(<$STR(S$时装升星材料名)>).DURA> $STR(N$时装升星材料所需数)
#ACT
TAKE $STR(S$时装升星材料名) $STR(N$时装升星材料所需数)
TABLE SZ_<$SCRIPTPARAM(1)> <$SCRIPTPARAM(2)> + 1
SENDMSG 19 <$STR(S$时装名)>升星成功
MOV S98 7758
GOTO @<$SCRIPTPARAM(6)>
GOTO @临时属性
CLEARVAR S98
BREAK
#ELSEACT
SENDMSG 19 <$STR(S$时装名)>(时装)不足
BREAK
